# Intro starting events and political machinations

country_event = { #Death of King George V
	id = french_republic_events.4
	title = french_republic_events.4.t
	desc = french_republic_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_death_george

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by the CAN event

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.4 option french_republic_events.4.a"
		name = french_republic_events.4.a #The King is dead, long live the king
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.5 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Lion in Canada
	id = french_republic_events.5
	title = french_republic_events.5.t
	desc = french_republic_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_edward2

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.5 option french_republic_events.5.a"
		name = french_republic_events.5.a #Time to return home
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = NFA_committed_to_return_home
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = NFA_committed_to_return_home
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.6 days = 14 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Book Competition - Setup
	id = french_republic_events.6
	title = french_republic_events.6.t
	desc = french_republic_events.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_books

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.6 option french_republic_events.6.a"
		name = french_republic_events.6.a #Let's see what they wrote
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.7 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { #Set up the variables for the power struggle
			set_variable = {
				var = Pet_influence
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Mor_influence
				value = 2
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Pet_corruption
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Competition_Loop_Counter
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Book Competition - Books
	id = french_republic_events.7
	title = french_republic_events.7.t
	desc = french_republic_events.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_books

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.7 option french_republic_events.7.a"
		name = french_republic_events.7.a #Support Mordacq
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.8 days = 10 }
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.7 option french_republic_events.7.b"
		name = french_republic_events.7.b #Support CdG
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SUS_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.9 days = 10 }
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.7 option french_republic_events.7.c"
		name = french_republic_events.7.c #Let it run it's course
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SUS_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.10 days = 10 }
			set_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Franchet d'Espèrey Retires
	id = french_republic_events.13
	title = french_republic_events.13.t
	desc = french_republic_events.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_TheOtherMarshal

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.13 option french_republic_events.13.a"
		name = french_republic_events.13.a #Pass the Torch to the Bear
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey }
			retire_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey
		}
		NFA_henri_mordacq = { promote_leader = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.16 days = 15 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.13 option french_republic_events.13.b"
		name = french_republic_events.13.b #Lion Undivided
		ai_chance = {
			base = 32
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SUS_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0 }
			set_country_flag = Petain_headstart_cf #Gives Petain a slight boost in the Fight for Influence
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey }
			retire_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.19 days = 15 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.13 option french_republic_events.13.c"
		name = french_republic_events.13.c #Young Guard
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SUS_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_path option = NFA_PATH_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey }
			retire_character = NFA_louis_franchet_desperey
		}
		NFA_charles_de_gaulle = { promote_leader = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.43 days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

		}

country_event = { #Put Mordacq in charge
	id = french_republic_events.17
	title = french_republic_events.17.t
	desc = french_republic_events.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_NFA_Mordacq

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.17 option french_republic_events.17.a"
		name = french_republic_events.17.a #Général, bienvenue!
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = NFA_philippe_petain }
			retire_character = NFA_philippe_petain
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		activate_advisor = NFA_francois_de_la_rocque_sic
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.89 days = 25 }
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.91 days = 13 } #Trouble in the Garrison
		}
	}
}

	id = french_republic_events.96
	immediate = {

	}
	title = french_republic_events.96.t
	desc = french_republic_events.96.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.96 option french_republic_events.96.a"
		name = french_republic_events.96.a #Vive La Republique!
		add_political_power = 25
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_union_sacree_coalition_tooltip
		activate_advisor = NFA_francois_de_la_rocque_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.25
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NFA.coalition_stability = 0.25 }
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.97 days = 14 }
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.270 days = 40 random_days = 50 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc_lar = yes }
				NFA_create_george_groussard_operative = yes
			}
			NFA_henri_mordacq = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
					promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = NFA_henri_mordacq_dem_leader_desc
							ideology = social_conservative_subtype
							traits = { NFA_Bear_Elect }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = NATFRA_Democracy_Restored
			random_other_country = { news_event = french_republic_news_events.3 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen }
				clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
				NFA_remove_de_gaulle_military_ideas = yes
				set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen }
				set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
	}
}

					max = 30

		}

country_event = { #Competition Counter
	id = french_republic_events.28
	title = french_republic_events.28.t
	desc = french_republic_events.28.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.28 option french_republic_events.28.a"
		name = french_republic_events.28.a
		if = { #Loop Again
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Competition_Loop_Counter
					value = 1
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = Mordacq_Airwaves
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NATFRA_CSN
					has_country_flag = NATFRA_Democracy_Restored
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
						has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
				NFA_remove_de_gaulle_military_ideas = yes
				clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
				set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
			}
			#Do nothing to end the loop
		}
		else = { #Someone is a Winner
			clr_country_flag = Fight_for_influence_on
			if = { #Check if Mordacq has more influence than Petain
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = Mor_influence
						value = Pet_influence
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = french_republic_events.35 days = 7 } # Mordacq coups Petain
				set_country_flag = NFA_Napoleon_0
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = french_republic_events.39 days = 15 } # Petain has more influence
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Corruption Check
	id = french_republic_events.30
	title = french_republic_events.30.t
	desc = french_republic_events.30.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.30 option french_republic_events.30.a"
		name = french_republic_events.30.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 6
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.32 days = 1 } # Corruption still coming
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NFA_event_31
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 5
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 3
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.31 days = 1 } # High Corruption warning
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.30 days = 7 } #Loop the checker
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf
				has_country_flag = Fight_for_influence_on
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.30 days = 7 } #Loop the checker
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # GER invites us to discuss the occupation of France
	id = french_republic_events.120
	title = french_republic_events.120.t
	desc = french_republic_events.120.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_map_france

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Meet with the Germans
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.120 option french_republic_events.120.a"
		name = french_republic_events.120.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 4
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = french_republic_events.134 } #The French enter negotiations - Case 1
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 3
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = french_republic_events.132 } #The French enter negotiations - Case 2
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 2
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = french_republic_events.130 } #The French enter negotiations - Case 3
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 1
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = french_republic_events.128 } #The French enter negotiations - Case 4
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 0
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = french_republic_events.125 } #The French enter negotiations - Case 5
		}
	}

	option = { #Do not fall for the trick
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.120 option french_republic_events.120.b"

		GER = { country_event = french_republic_events.121 } #The French decline talks
	}

	}
	desc = {
		text = french_republic_events.125.d.5.wal #Wallonia is an ally with GER
		trigger = { WAL = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = french_republic_events.125.d.5.nobel #Belgium nor Wallonia is an ally with GER
		trigger = { GER_has_Belgian_Ally = no }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Push the hawks plan
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.125 option french_republic_events.125.a"
		name = french_republic_events.125.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ai = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				surrender_progress > 0.3
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = { GER_has_Belgian_Ally = yes }
			set_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_4
		}
		else = {
			set_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_4_nobel
		}
		set_global_flag = GER_pushed_peace_deal
		NFA = { country_event = french_republic_events.127 } #French receive case deal 4
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_Hawk_Warning_tt
	}

	option = { #The moderate plan
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.125 option french_republic_events.125.b"
		name = french_republic_events.125.b
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_5
		NFA = { country_event = french_republic_events.126 } #French receive case deal 5
	}
}

	desc = french_republic_events.223.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_delaRocque_speech

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.223 option french_republic_events.223.a"
		name = french_republic_events.223.a #Some semblance of Democracy
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = NFA_election option = NFA_ELECTION_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea_with_trait = KR_parliament_sic } }
			activate_advisor = NFA_national_assembly_sic
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_tt_PSF_becomes_ade
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value = party_popularity@social_conservative }
			set_temp_variable = { NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse = 0 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { var = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse value = party_popularity@social_conservative }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value_reverse }
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = NFA_conservative_to_liberal_value }
			NFA_francois_de_la_rocque = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
					promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = NFA_francois_de_la_rocque_leader_desc
							ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
							traits = { NFA_Colonel }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NATFRA_semblance_of_democracy_cf
	}

	option = {

					limit = { has_ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
					promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = NFA_louis_marin_leader_desc
							ideology = social_conservative_subtype
							traits = { NFA_Professor }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea_with_trait = KR_parliament_sic } }
			activate_advisor = NFA_national_assembly_sic
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.234 days = 1460 } #Loop the Legislative Reelections
		}
	}
}

		name = french_republic_events.251.a #Let us continue our efforts to incorporate African peoples as French Citizens
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = NATFRA_Civ_Mission }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = 0.075
		swap_ideas = {

	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.251 option french_republic_events.251.b"
		name = french_republic_events.251.b #Continue widesweeping autonomy across the country
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = NATFRA_Promote_Autonomy }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 75
		add_stability = 0.05
		set_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_Algiers_Conference_AF_effect
		remove_ideas = NFA_native_unrest_4
		hidden_effect = {
			# French Saharan Africa #

						state = 700 #Sierra Leone
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance
				}
				clr_state_flag = nfa_state_colonial_resistance_flag
				clear_variable = NFA_colonial_resistance_target_var
				clear_variable = NFA_colonial_resistance_compliance_var

				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Autonomous_State }
				force_enable_resistance = { occupier = NFA clear = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.316 option french_republic_events.316.b"
		name = french_republic_events.316.b
		add_to_variable = {
			var = NFA_AF_purged_medium
			value = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.316 option french_republic_events.316.c"
		name = french_republic_events.316.c
		add_to_variable = {
			var = NFA_AF_purged_high
			value = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Conclusion of the Purge chain
	id = french_republic_events.317
	title = french_republic_events.317.t
	desc = french_republic_events.317.d
	picture = GFX_AF_trial_dec_1

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.317 option french_republic_events.317.a"
		name = french_republic_events.317.a #A new bonus
		remove_ideas = NFA_republican_remnants
		set_country_flag = NFA_AF_purge_decisions_over
		if = { #Give the idea of the most clicked option
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_low > NFA_AF_purged_high
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_low > NFA_AF_purged_medium
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_low_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_medium > NFA_AF_purged_low
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_medium > NFA_AF_purged_high
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_medium_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_high > NFA_AF_purged_low
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_high > NFA_AF_purged_medium
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_high_idea
		}
		# If there is a tie situation
		else = {
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_medium_idea
		}
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_low
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_medium
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_high
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to check if post-war events can fire, depending on owned states and months
	id = french_republic_events.529

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.529 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 762 #Nice
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.518 days = 8 random_days = 48 } #Restoration of Monaco
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 21 #Marseille
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.8.29
						date < 1939.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.8.29
						date < 1940.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.8.29
						date < 1941.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.8.29
						date < 1942.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.8.29
						date < 1943.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.8.29
						date < 1944.10.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.530 days = 2 } #Festival d'Avignon
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.179 days = 95 } #The question of Montmartre
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.531 days = 450 } #A mosque in Paris?
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.6.29
						date < 1939.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.6.29
						date < 1940.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.6.29
						date < 1941.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.6.29
						date < 1942.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.6.29
						date < 1943.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.6.29
						date < 1944.8.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.532 days = 2 } #First New Tour de France
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.1.29
						date < 1939.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.1.29
						date < 1940.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.1.29
						date < 1941.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.1.29
						date < 1942.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.1.29
						date < 1943.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.1.29
						date < 1944.2.25
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.540 days = 2 } #Emmaus
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 15 #Normandy
			}
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.533 days = 160 } #Rouen Reconstruction
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.534 days = 250 } #Tank in Vimoutiers
		}
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.529 days = 45 } #Loop the event without jumping over months
	}
}

# French Guinea and Upper Volta

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - French Guinea
	id = french_republic_events.443

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			806 = { #Guinea
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			808 = { #Upper Volta
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF }
	}

	option = { #Mission Attacked - 444
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.443 option 1"
		trigger = {
			806 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } #Guinea
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.34
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
		country_event = french_republic_events.444
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.443 days = 108 random_days = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Volta kings dispute - 471
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.443 option 2"
		trigger = {
			808 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
				808 = { is_core_of = ROOT } #Upper Volta
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.125
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
		country_event = french_republic_events.471
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.443 days = 108 random_days = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Infrastructure Sabotaged - 445
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.443 option 3"
		trigger = {
			806 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Upper Volta
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked }

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
		}
		country_event = french_republic_events.445
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.443 days = 144 random_days = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Garrison Attacked - 446
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.443 option 4"
		trigger = {
			808 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 808 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Upper Volta
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute }
			}
		}

	}
	option = { #no effect

			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.16

	trigger = {
		557 = { #Mauritania
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
			NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF }
	}

	option = { #Bedouin Raid - 453
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.452 option 1"
		trigger = {
			557 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			967 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		country_event = french_republic_events.453
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.452 days = 208 random_days = 172 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Burnt Village - 454
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.452 option 2"
		trigger = {
			557 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			967 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 32 }
		set_country_flag = nfa_burnt_village
		country_event = french_republic_events.454
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.452 days = 208 random_days = 172 } #loop
	}

	option = { #no effect
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.452 option 3"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 37
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.89
				has_country_flag = nfa_burnt_village
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = nfa_burnt_village }
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.452 days = 108 random_days = 96 } # Nothing happens
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = french_republic_events.452 days = 208 random_days = 96 } # Nothing happens
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - Senegal

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
			has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.467 days = 158 random_days = 36 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Miner strike - 468

				factor = 1.4

			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
		country_event = french_republic_events.470
	}

	option = { #Nothing happens
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.467 option 4"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.08
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike

# Revolt events from french_republic_events.600
#####

country_event = { #Colony Revolts (donotlog)
	id = french_republic_events.601
	title = french_republic_events.601.t
	desc = french_republic_events.601.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOM_intro

	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					event_target:revolter = { tag = CHA }
					has_game_rule = { rule = CHA_revolt option = CHA_REVOLT_NO }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					event_target:revolter = { tag = NGR }
					has_game_rule = { rule = NGR_revolt option = NGR_REVOLT_NO }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					event_target:revolter = { tag = VOL }
					has_game_rule = { rule = VOL_revolt option = VOL_REVOLT_NO }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					event_target:revolter = { tag = MLI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = MLI_revolt option = MLI_REVOLT_NO }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					event_target:revolter = { tag = GNA }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GNA_revolt option = GNA_REVOLT_NO }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					event_target:revolter = { tag = MRT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = MRT_revolt option = MRT_REVOLT_NO }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					event_target:revolter = { tag = TUN }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TUN_revolt option = TUN_REVOLT_NO }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					event_target:revolter = { tag = IVO }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IVO_revolt option = IVO_REVOLT_NO }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { always = yes }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NFA_active_rebellion
			set_country_flag = NFA_rebelled_@event_target:revolter
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = NFA_crush_resistance target = event_target:revolter }
			event_target:revolter = {
				log = "KR_Event_Logging;[THIS.GetTag] REVOLTS AGAINST NFA"
				every_core_state = {
					limit = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
					teleport_armies = { limit = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
					transfer_state_to = event_target:revolter
				}
				NFA_spawn_revolt_armies = yes
				every_controlled_state = {
					every_neighbor_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
							has_resistance = yes
						}
						add_resistance = 8
						add_compliance = -4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = french_republic_events.601.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NFA_small_native_revolt
				NFA_has_multiple_african_revolts = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_revolts_getting_out_of_hand
			remove_ideas = NFA_small_native_revolt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with_major = no #Don't add the idea if during 2WK
				NFA_has_multiple_african_revolts = no #Don't add the idea if NFA has lots of revolts
				NOT = { has_idea = NFA_small_native_revolt } #Don't add the idea twice
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_small_native_revolt
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:revolter
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = french_republic_events.601.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -75
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Colonial_Exploitation }
				}
			}
			add_resistance = 12
		}
	}
}

			limit = {

					has_war_with = MOR
				}

			}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 290 #The Rif
						state = 699 #Rio de Oro
						state = 968 #Ifni
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = MOR
			}
		}

		### Events
		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {

						is_ai = no
						has_war_with = EGY
					}
					EGY = {
						is_subject = no
						OR = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
							is_in_faction = no
						}
					}
				}
				ENT = {
					country_event = { id = french_republic_events.625 days = 1 } #Do you want to continue the war?
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ENT = {
						is_ai = yes
						has_war_with = EGY
					}
					EGY = {
						is_subject = no
						OR = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
							is_in_faction = no
						}
					}
				}
				EGY = {
					country_event = { id = french_republic_events.626 days = 2 } #ENT sues for peace
				}
			}
		}

		### Peace off the rebels
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				is_valid_peace_target = yes
				OR = {
					tag = TUN
					tag = CHA
					tag = NGR
					tag = MLI
					tag = MRT
					tag = VOL
					tag = GNA
					tag = IVO
					tag = SEN
					tag = SIE
				}
			}
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
			ROOT = {
				clr_country_flag = NFA_active_rebellion
				clr_country_flag = NFA_rebelled_@PREV
			}
		}

		### Free all puppets
		every_subject_country = {
			overlord = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}

		### Kill Off NFA
		force_capitulate = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to force the resistance modifier to go back on NFA states that glitch out and don't get the modifier added
	id = french_republic_events.633
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		NFA = {
			every_owned_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = nfa_state_colonial_resistance_flag
						NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance } }
						NOT = { is_core_of = NFA }
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = nfa_state_colonial_exploitation_flag
						NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Colonial_Exploitation } }
						NOT = { is_core_of = NFA }
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Colonial_Exploitation }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.633 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a #Drat
	}
}

	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
		OR = {
			has_game_rule = { rule = CHA_revolt option = CHA_REVOLT_YES }
			has_game_rule = { rule = NGR_revolt option = NGR_REVOLT_YES }
			has_game_rule = { rule = VOL_revolt option = VOL_REVOLT_YES }
			has_game_rule = { rule = MLI_revolt option = MLI_REVOLT_YES }
			has_game_rule = { rule = GNA_revolt option = GNA_REVOLT_YES }
			has_game_rule = { rule = MRT_revolt option = MRT_REVOLT_YES }
			has_game_rule = { rule = TUN_revolt option = TUN_REVOLT_YES }
			has_game_rule = { rule = IVO_revolt option = IVO_REVOLT_YES }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.634 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a #Drat
		trigger = { threat > 0.7 }
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.635 days = 3 random_days = 2 }	# CHA
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.636 days = 6 random_days = 2 }	# NGR
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.637 days = 9 random_days = 2 }	# VOL
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.638 days = 12 random_days = 2 }	# MLI
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.639 days = 15 random_days = 2 }	# GNA
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.640 days = 18 random_days = 2 }	# MRT
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.641 days = 21 random_days = 2 }	# TUN
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.642 days = 24 random_days = 2 }	# IVO
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_events.634 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a #Drat
		trigger = { NOT = { threat > 0.7 } }
		country_event = { id = french_republic_events.634 days = 25 random_days = 10 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to force CHA revolt
	id = french_republic_events.635
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
		has_game_rule = { rule = CHA_revolt option = CHA_REVOLT_YES }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NFA_rebelled_CHA }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NFA_previously_rebelled_CHA }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

		name = KR.hidden.a #Drat
		CHA = { save_event_target_as = revolter }
		country_event = french_republic_events.601
	}

	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_news_events.1" }
	title = french_republic_news_events.1.t
	desc = french_republic_news_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_OTT_buraimi

	major = yes
	fire_for_sender = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			regional_africa_news = yes
			regional_europe_news = yes
			tag = CAN
		}
	}

		name = french_republic_news_events.1.a

			has_socialist_government = yes
		}

# France Declares a Fourth Republic
news_event = {
	id = french_republic_news_events.9
	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event french_republic_news_events.9" }
	title = french_republic_news_events.9.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NFA = { has_liberal_government = yes }
		}
		text = french_republic_news_events.9.d.libs
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NFA = { has_government = social_conservative }
		}
		text = french_republic_news_events.9.d.cons
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NFA = { has_authoritarian_government = yes }
		}
		text = french_republic_news_events.9.d.gamer
	}

	picture = GFX_news_event_NFA_return_marseille
	fire_for_sender = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	option = { # For a prosperous tomorrow!
		name = french_republic_news_events.9.a
		trigger = {
			tag = NFA
		}
	}
	option = { # A welcoming development!
		name = french_republic_news_events.9.b
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = NFA
			NOT = {
				tag = NFA
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # A familiar neighbor returns.
		name = french_republic_news_events.9.c
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
		}
	}
	option = { # Europe is lost...
		name = french_republic_news_events.9.e
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Interesting.
		name = french_republic_news_events.9.f
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = NFA
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
